<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:new.html>New</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">critērium</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κριτήριον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kritḗrion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***cultuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cultuur.html>cultuur</a> (4262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:culture.html>culture</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cultivation; <a href = vnd.unilang:culture.html>culture</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cultūra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cultivation; <a href = vnd.unilang:culture.html>culture</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultus.html>cultus</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">colō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:till.html>till</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:cultivate.html>cultivate</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:worship.html>worship</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">colōnus</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">colōnia</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:move.html>move</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:turn.html>turn</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:around.html>around</a>)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***curare.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:curare.html>curare</a> (70540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:curare.html>curare</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
